<p>प्रमुख विशेषज्ञों के साथ MATHWORKS द्वारा प्रदान किया जाने वाला यह फ्री-टू-ऑडिट पाठ्यक्रम व्यावहारिक और उद्योग-उन्मुख सामग्री के साथ डेटा विज्ञान में MATLAB की शक्ति को समझने में आपकी सहायता करेगा।</p> <p>पोस्ट <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-exploratory-data-analysis-matlab/">सीखें कि एक डेटा वैज्ञानिक की तरह कैसे सोचें: एक समीक्षा MATLAB के साथ अन्वेषणात्मक डेटा विश्लेषण</a> पहले <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">क्लास सेंट्रल द्वारा रिपोर्ट</a> पर दिखाई दिया।</p> <h2><img Loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85360" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Exploratory- डेटा-विश्लेषण-साथ-MATLAB-Erin-Byrne-course-instructor.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content /uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-Erin-Byrne-course-instructor.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/ एक्सप्लोरेटरी-डेटा-एनालिसिस-विद-मैटलैब-एरिन-बायर्न-कोर्स-इंस्ट्रक्टर-300x150.png 300w, /></h2> <h2>परिचय</h2> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exploratory-data-analysis-matlab-17125">MATLAB के साथ अन्वेषणात्मक डेटा विश्लेषण</a>, मैथवर्क्स द्वारा कौरसेरा के माध्यम से पेश किया गया, इनमें से एक है सबसे व्यावहारिक और उद्योग-उन्मुख पाठ्यक्रम जो मैंने वेब पर लिए हैं। यह कोर्स <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/practical-data-science-matlab-18864">MATLAB के साथ प्रैक्टिकल डेटा साइंस</a> नामक विशेषज्ञता कार्यक्रम का हिस्सा है, जिसमें चार शामिल हैं इस विषय पर पाठ्यक्रम। संपूर्ण विशेषज्ञता को पूरा होने में लगभग पांच महीने लगेंगे। कई रूपों में डेटा का विश्लेषण करने के लिए मानक प्रक्रियाओं के माध्यम से उपस्थित लोगों का मार्गदर्शन करने के लिए विशेषज्ञता का विषय अच्छी तरह से डिज़ाइन किया गया है।</p> <h2>मैंने यह कोर्स क्यों किया</h2> <figure id="attachment_85361" aria-describeby="caption-attachment-85361" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img Loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image -85361" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-4th-module-statistical-analysis.png" alt= "" चौड़ाई = "1024" ऊंचाई = "512" srcset = "https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-4th-module -statistical-analysis.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-4th-module-statistical-analysis-300x150। png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-4th-module-statistical-analysis-768x384.png 768w" size= "(अधिकतम-चौड़ाई: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85361" class="wp-caption-text">मॉड्यूल 4 से, सांख्यिकीय विश्लेषण।</figcaption></figure> <p>हम एक ऐसे युग में रहते हैं जहां प्रतिदिन बड़ी मात्रा में डेटा उत्पन्न होता है। यह डेटा ट्रैफ़िक, कृषि, इंटरनेट ऑफ़ थिंग्स, इंटरकनेक्टेड इलेक्ट्रिकल ग्रिड, ट्रांसपोर्ट और कई अन्य क्षेत्रों सहित कई स्रोतों से आता है। डेटा की बढ़ती मात्रा मनुष्यों के लिए एक चुनौती बन गई है क्योंकि हमारे दिमाग कम समय में तेजी से जटिल डेटा के बड़े हिस्से की गणना करने के लिए विकसित नहीं हुए हैं। दूसरी ओर, हमें महत्वपूर्ण स्थितियों और वित्तीय रूप से महत्वपूर्ण मामलों पर निर्णय लेने के लिए इस डेटा का समय पर और सटीक विश्लेषण करने की आवश्यकता है। एक इलेक्ट्रिकल इंजीनियर के रूप में, मैं देखता हूं कि प्रत्येक घंटे उपभोक्ताओं से कितना डेटा उत्पन्न होता है और मनुष्यों के लिए इसे स्वयं समझना कितना कठिन होता है। MATLAB, एक शक्तिशाली कम्प्यूटेशनल इंजन के रूप में इस डेटा का विश्लेषण करने में हमारी मदद करने की क्षमता रखता है और इसके अलावा, इस डोमेन में मॉडल को प्रशिक्षित करने के लिए कृत्रिम बुद्धिमत्ता का उपयोग करता है। मेरा विशिष्ट लक्ष्य डेटा विज्ञान में अपने कौशल को विकसित करना और विद्युत शक्ति नेटवर्क योजना के विश्लेषण में मदद करने के लिए इसका उपयोग करना था। हमें निम्नलिखित कार्यों को सफलतापूर्वक करने की आवश्यकता है:</p> <ओल> <li>    छोटी और लंबी अवधि के अंतराल में उपभोक्ताओं के व्यवहार की भविष्यवाणी करें,</li> <li>    अक्षय ऊर्जा उत्पादन की योजना बनाने के लिए मौसम के मिजाज का अनुमान लगाएं,</li> <li>    लागत प्रभावी तरीके से आपूर्ति और मांग को संतुलित करने के लिए उत्पादन की योजना बनाएं,</li> <li>    नेटवर्क की बाधाओं, भीड़भाड़ के समय और बिंदुओं आदि की पहचान करने के लिए उपभोक्ताओं के डेटा का विश्लेषण करें।</li> </ओल> <h2>इतिहास</h2> <p>मुझे कौरसेरा प्लेटफॉर्म में पाठ्यक्रम मिला और क्लास सेंट्रल वेबसाइट में विशेषज्ञता में इसी तरह के और बाकी पाठ्यक्रमों की खोज की। कुछ सत्र लेने के बाद, सामग्री और पाठ्यक्रम कई मायनों में अद्वितीय साबित हुए और इसलिए मैंने इसे जारी रखा।</p> <h2>प्रशिक्षक</h2> <figure id="attachment_85362" aria-describeby="caption-attachment-85362" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img Loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85362 size -फुल" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-Instructors.png" alt="" width="1024 "ऊंचाई ="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-Instructors.png 1024w, https:// www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-Instructors-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content /uploads/2023/02/Exploratory-Data-Analysis-with-MATLAB-Instructors-768x384.png 768w" size="(अधिकतम-चौड़ाई: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85362 " class="wp-caption-text">कोर्स प्रशिक्षक, बाएं से दाएं: एडम फिलिओन, हीदर गोर्र, ब्रैंडन आर्मस्ट्रांग, और एरिन बर्न।</figcaption></figure> <p>मैंने <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/institution/mathworks">MathWorks</a> द्वारा पेश किए जाने वाले कई अन्य ऑनलाइन कार्यक्रमों और पाठ्यक्रमों में प्रशिक्षकों को देखा है और उनके पास बहुत गहरा है उनके द्वारा प्रस्तुत सामग्री का ज्ञान और अनुभव। मैं उनके द्वारा प्रदान की जाने वाली सामग्री में सैद्धांतिक और व्यावहारिक ज्ञान और संगठन दोनों देखता हूं जो पाठ्यक्रम को एक सुखद अनुभव बनाता है।</p> <h2>माई स्किल्स</h2> <p>मेरे पास अक्षय ऊर्जा इंजीनियरिंग में मास्टर डिग्री है और मेरा स्नातक इलेक्ट्रिकल इंजीनियरिंग में है। मैं अकादमी और मेरी नौकरी दोनों में MATLAB का उपयोगकर्ता रहा हूं। मैं वर्तमान में एक विशेषज्ञ इंजीनियर के रूप में काम करता हूं और डेटा विश्लेषण सहित विभिन्न समस्याओं को हल करने के लिए MATLAB को हमारे दैनिक उपकरणों में से एक के रूप में उपयोग करता हूं। मैंने पहले से ही मैथवर्क्स द्वारा एडएक्स के माध्यम से पेश किए जाने वाले अन्य डेटा साइंस पाठ्यक्रम भी ले लिए थे।</p> <h2>सफल कैसे बनें</h2> <p>पाठ्यक्रम से मेरे अनुभव के अनुसार, यदि पाठक के पास डेटा विज्ञान, गणित और/या इंजीनियरिंग में कुछ सैद्धांतिक पृष्ठभूमि है तो यह एक फायदा है। यह भी बहुत अच्छा है कि जब आप पाठ्यक्रम में सामग्री सीखते हैं तो ज्ञान को लागू करना शुरू करते हैं। हालाँकि, MATLAB होना आवश्यक है क्योंकि पाठ्यक्रम समाप्त होने के बाद ऑनलाइन संस्करण उपलब्ध नहीं होगा।</p> <p><i>संपादक की टिप्पणी: शिक्षार्थियों को सभी पाठ्यक्रमों के लिए MATLAB तक पहुंच प्रदान की जाती है।</i></p> <h2>प्रमाणपत्र</h2> <p>कोर्सेरा में अन्य MOOCs की तरह एक शुल्क के लिए पाठ्यक्रम एक प्रमाण पत्र प्रदान करता है। आप केवल पाठ्यक्रम या संपूर्ण विशेषज्ञता का चुनाव कर सकते हैं। कौरसेरा में कौरसेरा प्लस सदस्यता जैसे अन्य विकल्प हैं जहां आप हजारों पाठ्यक्रमों तक वार्षिक पहुंच प्राप्त कर सकते हैं और उनके लिए एक प्रमाण पत्र प्राप्त कर सकते हैं।</p> <h2>पाठ्यक्रम</h2> <p>यह कोर्स क्लास सेंट्रल की <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/collection/top-free-online-courses">अब तक के सर्वश्रेष्ठ मुफ़्त ऑनलाइन कोर्स</a> की सूची में है। यह सामग्री में समृद्ध है और पाँच सप्ताह में अच्छी तरह व्यवस्थित है। पाठ्यक्रम में एक मानक डेटा विज्ञान कार्य की सभी मूल बातें शामिल हैं। यह डेटा साइंस के वर्कफ़्लो का वर्णन करता है, डेटा कैसे आयात करें, इसे कैसे फ़िल्टर और सॉर्ट करें, डेटा पर आवश्यक विश्लेषण और गणना कैसे करें और अंत में इसे अपने दर्शकों के सामने कैसे प्रस्तुत करें। प्रतिभागी कई मंचों में विषयों पर चर्चा कर सकते हैं और प्रश्न पूछ सकते हैं।</p> <h2>ग्रेडिंग</h2> <p>कई ग्रेडेड और अनग्रेडेड क्विज़ और टेस्ट हैं। इस पाठ्यक्रम में सहायता के लिए मैथवर्क्स वेबसाइट के माध्यम से बहुत सारे अभ्यास परीक्षण भी प्रदान किए जाते हैं। प्रमाणपत्र के लिए विचार किए जाने के लिए ग्रेडेड टेस्ट पास करना आवश्यक है।</p> <h2>समय की प्रतिबद्धता</h2> <p>कोर्स में प्रति सप्ताह 4 घंटे समर्पित करने का सुझाव दिया गया है, हालांकि, यदि आप विषयों को गहराई से समझना चाहते हैं, तो आपको विषयों पर और अधिक शोध करने के लिए और अधिक समय की आवश्यकता होगी और अधिक महत्वपूर्ण रूप से उनका स्वयं अभ्यास करें।</p> <h2>निष्कर्ष</h2> <p>मैंने पाठ्यक्रम की सामग्री को सफलतापूर्वक पढ़ लिया और इसे बहुत उपयोगी पाया। डेटा साइंस में MATLAB की शक्ति को समझने में इसने वास्तव में मेरी बहुत मदद की। अब मैं सीखे गए विषयों का उपयोग अपने काम में कर सकता हूँ। यह मेरे द्वारा ऑनलाइन लिए गए सर्वोत्तम पाठ्यक्रमों में से एक है।</p> <p><em>संपादक की टिप्पणी: यहाँ विशेषज्ञता में तीसरे पाठ्यक्रम की गहन समीक्षा है, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-predictive-modeling-matlab/" >कोर्स रिव्यू: मैथवर्क्स द्वारा MATLAB के साथ प्रिडिक्टिव मॉडलिंग एंड मशीन लर्निंग</a> जिसे मागेश जॉन द्वारा लिखा गया है, एक प्रशिक्षक ब्रैंडन आर्मस्ट्रांग की टिप्पणी के साथ।</em></p> <p>पोस्ट <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-exploratory-data-analysis-matlab/">सीखें कि एक डेटा वैज्ञानिक की तरह कैसे सोचें: एक समीक्षा MATLAB के साथ अन्वेषणात्मक डेटा विश्लेषण</a> पहले <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">क्लास सेंट्रल द्वारा रिपोर्ट</a> पर दिखाई दिया।</p> हत्तपः://ववव.क्लाससेंट्रल.कॉम/रिपोर्ट/रिव्यु-एक्सप्लोरेटरी-डाटा-एनालिसिस-मतलब/फीड/ 0 aria-describeby="caption-attachment-85344" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img Loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image -85344" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Learning-to-teach_-mentoring-and-tutoring-student-teachers-The-difference.png" alt="" चौड़ाई="1024" ऊंचाई="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Learning-to-teach_-mentoring-and-tutoring -student-teachers-The-difference.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Learning-to-teach_-mentoring-and-tutoring-student-teachers- अंतर-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Learning-to-teach_-mentoring-and-tutoring-student-teachers-The-difference -768x384.png 768w" size="(अधिकतम-चौड़ाई: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85344" class="wp-caption-text">से "क्या अंतर है? ” पाठ 1.</figcaption></figure> <p>प्रशिक्षण बहुत अच्छी तरह से डिज़ाइन किया गया है। यह बहुत स्पष्ट है और मुझे यह इतना दिलचस्प लगा कि मैंने इसे "लगभग एक सांस में" पढ़ लिया। यह वही है जो मुझे चाहिए था और जिसकी मुझे तलाश थी। मैंने मेंटरिंग के बारे में बहुत कुछ सीखा। "संरक्षक" शब्द का अर्थ उस व्यक्ति से है जो अपने करियर की शुरुआत में एक शिक्षक के साथ दैनिक रूप से काम करता है, अपने कार्यकाल के दौरान उनके विकास का समर्थन करता है। मुझे उस शिक्षक की याद आई जिसने स्कूल में काम करना शुरू करने पर मेरा साथ दिया था।</p> <p>इस प्रशिक्षण में, एक संरक्षक की भूमिका में क्या महत्वपूर्ण है, विशिष्ट निर्देश और किन बातों पर ध्यान देना चाहिए, इसके बारे में दिशा-निर्देश स्पष्ट रूप से दिए गए थे, और यह कि एक संरक्षक की भूमिका में निस्वार्थ सलाह देने के साथ-साथ निरीक्षण करना भी शामिल है आपके छात्र की भावनाएं।</p> <p>मैंने यह भी सीखा है कि एक "ट्यूटर" की भूमिका में शैक्षणिक सहायता प्रदान करना शामिल हो सकता है, यदि कोई छात्र शैक्षणिक योग्यता के लिए अध्ययन कर रहा है, और शिक्षण का निरीक्षण करने के लिए स्कूल का दौरा कर रहा है। इस भूमिका के लिए भी स्पष्ट दिशानिर्देश हैं।</p> <h2>निष्कर्ष</h2> <figure id="attachment_85343" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85343" class="wp-caption-text">"मेंटर रोल" पाठ 2 से .</figcaption></figure> <p>मेरी राय में यह प्रशिक्षण है <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/openlearn-education-Development-learning-teach-me-95579">सीखना सीखना: छात्र शिक्षकों को सलाह देना और पढ़ाना< /a> बढ़िया, स्पष्ट है, इसमें अधिक समय की आवश्यकता नहीं है, और बहुत सारी जानकारी प्रदान करता है। मैं तहे दिल से इसकी सिफारिश उन सभी से करूंगा जो एक शिक्षक के काम में लगे हुए हैं।</p> <p>यह कोर्स मुझे अपने छात्रों के लिए एक बेहतर गुरु बनने में मदद करेगा, साथ ही छात्रों के लिए एक बेहतर शिक्षक भी। इस कोर्स के बाद मेरे पास मेंटर की भूमिका के बारे में एक स्पष्ट विचार है।</p> <h2>आगे क्या है</h2> <p>एक संबंधित पाठ्यक्रम जिसमें मैं भाग लेना चाहता हूं href="https://www.blackmagicdesign.com/products/davinciresolve/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Blackmagic Design</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> says on their website:</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">“DaVinci Resolve is the world’s only solution that combines editing, color correction, visual effects, motion graphics and audio post production all in one software tool!”</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This means that you don’t have to learn and use multiple applications for different post production tasks – you can carry out the entire process in DaVinci Resolve itself, faster and at a higher quality.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">DaVinci Resolve (originally da Vinci Resolve) was developed by da Vinci Systems in 2003 which was later on acquired by Blackmagic Design in 2009. The commercial version of the software is known as DaVinci Resolve Studio, while its free version (with reduced functionality) is simply called DaVinci Resolve.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">With DaVinci Resolve, you get DaVinci’s Emmy award winning image technology with 32‑bit float processing, patented YRGB color science, a wide gamut color space for HDR workflows. and Fairlight audio processing for the best in class sound.</span></p> <h3>Why are DaVinci Resolve Skills Important?</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">DaVinci Resolve is a popular choice for creating visual effects and motion graphics, as well as post-production workflows. As such, professionals who have skills in this software are in high demand in the industry.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">DaVinci Resolve is considered one of the </span><a href="https://crumplepop.com/davinci-resolve-vs-premiere-pro/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">leading video editing software</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> in a market that’s projected to reach a value of </span><a href="https://www.globenewswire.com/en/news-release/2022/09/14/2516320/0/en/Video-Editing-Software-Market-Size-is-projected-to-reach-USD-3-24-Billion-by-2030-growing-at-a-CAGR-of-5-6-Straits-Research.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">USD 3.24 Billion by 2030</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">. It&#8217;s a popular choice among professional editors and colorists in the film, television, and video production industry.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The job market for professionals with skills in DaVinci Resolve is generally strong, as the software is widely used in the film and television industry, you can easily find job openings on </span><a href="https://www.linkedin.com/jobs/davinci-resolve-jobs/?currentJobId=3306260142" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">LinkedIn</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, </span><a href="https://www.indeed.com/jobs?q=Full+Time+Davinci+Resolve+Editor&amp;from=mobRdr&amp;utm_source=%2Fm%2F&amp;utm_medium=redir&amp;utm_campaign=dt&amp;vjk=363afcf58c523bb8" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Indeed</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, and </span><a href="https://www.upwork.com/freelance-jobs/da-vinci-resolve/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Upwork</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> with an average salary of USD 54,946 in US, according to </span><a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/Salaries/video-editor-salary-SRCH_KO0,12.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Glassdoor</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">. However, the level of competition for jobs can vary depending on the specific role and location. Generally, the more specialized and in-demand the role, the higher the competition.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Having skills in DaVinci Resolve is an important asset for any professional in the video editing industry, but it is not the only skill that is needed to get a job. Employers also look for candidates who have a solid understanding of the technical aspects of video editing, such as color correction, visual effects, and audio mixing, as well as experience working on real-world projects. Additionally, a strong portfolio and a good understanding of the industry are important factors when looking for a job.</span></p> <h3>What is My Experience with DaVinci Resolve?</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I am a </span><a href="https://www.coursera.org/instructor/archisha-bhar" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Guided Project Instructor</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and a Beta Tester at Coursera, having tested many courses before they’re officially launched. logic programming language that’s mainly used for artificial intelligence, natural language processing, and symbolic computation. It’s based on first-order logic, which means that programs in Prolog consist of logical statements that are interpreted as facts or rules (for example, the premise ‘If it rains, then the ground is wet’ and ‘It is raining’ lead to the conclusion ‘The ground is wet’).</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">These facts and rules can be used to make logical deductions which can help in developing intelligent systems that can reason, learn, and solve problems using logical rules and data, such as in complex decision making systems and AI.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this guide, I’ve picked the best free online courses to learn Prolog. programmers</span></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h2>What is Prolog?</h2> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Prolog, short for Programming Logic, is a declarative programming language that was first developed in 1972 by Alain Colmerauer and Philippe Roussel. It is unique in that it is homoiconic, meaning it treats code as data, and is focused on specifying what you want to achieve rather than how to achieve it. This makes it well-suited for artificial intelligence and natural language processing tasks, as it allows the programmer to define a set of facts and rules that describe a problem and then use these to find a solution, or in other words, to ‘reason’.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Prolog is not only used in academia though, it has also seen commercial applications. The </span><a href="https://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se10/jvms10.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Java Virtual Machine Specification contains Prolog</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, </span><a href="https://github.com/nasa/MINX" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">NASA uses Prolog for voice-control</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, </span><a href="https://www.cs.nmsu.edu/ALP/2011/03/natural-language-processing-with-prolog-in-the-ibm-watson-system/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">IBM Watson’s natural language processing abilities come from Prolog</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, </span><a href="https://dtai.cs.kuleuven.be/CHR/files/Elston_SecuritEase.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">New Zealand’s stock broking system is written in Prolog</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, and a third of all airline tickets are handled by Prolog.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">While Prolog has been around for more than half a century now, that hasn’t stopped it from evolving, with more declarative features that make it easier to understand and use to create general programs with less effort. If you need to model and solve complex problems through symbolic data and logical deductions, a logical programming language like Prolog can save the day.</span></p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79248 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2.png" alt="Find your next course." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <h2>Best Courses Guides Methodology</h2> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous Best Courses Guides (</span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">you can find them all here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">). One course makes use of text and video formats.</span></li> <li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Two of the courses are interactive in the browser — no installation required!</span></li> </ul> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Without further ado, let’s go through the top picks.</span></p> <h2 id="anchor-1">1. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-the-power-of-prolog-120174" target="_blank" rel="noopener">The Power of Prolog (Markus Triska)</a></h2> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85331" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-The-Power-of-Prolog-Markus-Triska.png" alt="" width="1536" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-The-Power-of-Prolog-Markus-Triska.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-The-Power-of-Prolog-Markus-Triska-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-The-Power-of-Prolog-Markus-Triska-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-The-Power-of-Prolog-Markus-Triska-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My number one course for the best Prolog course is </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-the-power-of-prolog-120174" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Power of Prolog</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> course is my top pick because it is the most comprehensive and up-to-date course on Prolog that I have found. It has been consistently updated for two decades, so you can rest assured that you’re learning the latest modern features of the Prolog language. </span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course covers a wide range of topics, including simple integer arithmetic, web applications, theorem proving, and even artificial intelligence! In addition to its comprehensive course material, there are also </span><a href="https://www.metalevel.at/prolog/showcases/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">sample programs</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> for you to practice with </span><a href="https://www.metalevel.at/prolog/videos/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">and video tutorials</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> to help guide your learning. You’ll understand that Prolog is based on a subset of classical first-order predicate logic called </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horn_clause" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Horn clauses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> which allows for the proving of theorems through </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Resolution_(logic)" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">resolution</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> — an amazing tool for solving complex problems!</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Once you have the fundamentals of logic under your belt, you’ll soon be writing and reading Prolog programs. First, you’ll learn the most basic concepts of Prolog, such as its program and data structures. From there, you’ll learn how to reason effectively with Prolog by reading and writing Prolog programs, including doing integer arithmetic, sorting, and searching. You’ll level up your Prolog skills by exploring more advanced concepts such as logical purity and definite clause grammars, as well as practical techniques like declarative testing and debugging that can truly be a life-saver.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The potential of Prolog is truly limitless — from web applications, to databases, to cryptography, and of course, building artificial intelligence. Why is Prolog used for these? It’s because Prolog can emulate the process behind human decision making, proving complex mathematical theorems, and solving logic puzzles. You’ll find out how Prolog does this, as well how it is used in all of these applications in detail.</span></p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course consists of 33 chapters. /></span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My second pick for the best Prolog course is </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-simply-logical-120173" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Simply Logical – Intelligent Reasoning by Example</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> course focuses on Prolog programming in the context of Artificial Intelligence, implementing intelligent behavior in machines, and Computational Logic, automating various kinds of reasoning. The course&#8217;s philosophy is ‘teaching by showing, learning by doing’, which is reflected in the interactive code blocks embedded in the course page for you to experiment with. By the end of this course, you’ll understand how logic can be used to solve problems in AI.</span></p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is divided into 3 parts: Logic and Logic Programming; Reasoning with structured knowledge; Advanced reasoning techniques.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The first part serves as an introduction to Logic Programming with Prolog, where you’ll deal with concepts such as program clauses, query answering, proof trees, and recursive data structures in an intuitive manner. Then, you’ll cover them much more formally by proving soundness and completeness in a program. You’ll also uncover common Prolog programming techniques, including the use of SLD-trees, arithmetic expressions, second-order predicates, and programming techniques.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In Part II, the focus shifts to Artificial Intelligence concepts, specifically structured knowledge. You’ll learn how to represent structured knowledge (relationships) as graphs, and how to answer a problem with no known analytic solutions through two kinds of search — blind and informed.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Part III will explore advanced reasoning techniques beyond the boundaries of clausal logic, where sequences of events are happening over time, where truth is not guaranteed, and knowledge is available in non-logical form such as pictures or spoken text. You’ll learn how to turn natural language into clausal logics, and how to reason with incomplete information, and finally how to conduct inductive reasoning through generalization or specialization.</span></p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course consists of 12 chapters in total. You’ll learn by reading through chapter material, playing around with the interactive code samples, and completing the exercises given, some of them having answers.</span></p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>Institution</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">Simply Logical</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Website</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">book.simply-logical.space</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Author</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">Peter Flach</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Level</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">Beginner</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Workload</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">N/A</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Certificate</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">None</span></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h3>Fun Facts</h3> <ul> <li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">About Simply Logical is an open-source project providing a suite of online resources about Artificial Intelligence and Logic Programming with Prolog.</span></li> <li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Peter Flach is a Professor of Artificial Intelligence at the University of Bristol. You’ll delve into the basics of running and compiling basic prolog code and understand how facts like “The sky is blue” are represented as simple predicates in Prolog. Next, you’ll learn how to define rules that make use of these facts, such as &#8220;If the sky is blue and the sun is shining, then it is a nice day&#8221;. Then, you’ll see Prolog do something magical — give it a query like “Is it a nice day?” and watch as it determines the answer for you!</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Moving on, you’ll dive into representing information as variable syntax and structs, and figure out how to ask more sophisticated questions about the data you have. Arithmetic operations will become second nature as you see how Prolog performs them. And that’s just the beginning! You&#8217;ll learn about Prolog’s support for complex data structures, such as lists and pairs, and how to perform advanced operations like sorting and searching through lists to get the information you need.</span></p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course is 1–2 hours long and consists of 4 parts. You’ll learn how to use Prolog to describe facts and relationships about problems to facilitate automated reasoning.</span></p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Prolog is a programming language that enables you to describe facts and relationships about problems rather than merely outlining a series of steps to solve them. You’ll learn how to define facts and rules to facilitate automated reasoning, and use variables as a placeholder for values that might change. Then, you’ll learn how to use if statements to create complex terms and rules.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Prolog also has logical and arithmetic operators. You’ll learn how to use them, both sequentially as well as recursively. You’ll also see how you can read and write to consoles and files. In fact, one of the things you’ll discuss is how to modify the database of facts and rules directly. Finally, you’ll learn how to create lists in Prolog to represent more similarity-related values and work with strings.</span></p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course is 1 hour long. is a </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> collection of problems aimed to help students practice their logic programming skills in Prolog, where your goal should be to find the most elegant or logically clear solution of the given problems. Problems are marked by their difficulty, from easiest to hardest. </span></p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The collection is structured into seven sections:<br /> </span></p> <ol> <li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Prolog Lists: Manipulating lists in Prolog. Example questions:</span> <ul> <li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="2"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Find the last but one element of a list.</span></li> <li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="2"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Drop every N&#8217;th element from a list.</span></li> </ul> </li> <li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Arithmetic: Primes, mathematical algorithms, and functions. <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you’re primarily familiar with SQL, then thinking of Prolog as a relational database query language might be a great way to get started. That’s what this </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> course is about.</span></p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-an-introduction-to-prolog-for-sql-programers-120170" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">An introduction to Prolog for SQL programmers</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> teaches Prolog by simulating basic SQL operations through Prolog code, from querying to modifying databases.</span></p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course is made up of three parts.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The first part walks you through querying databases where you simulate traditional SQL commands like SELECT, INSERT, WHERE, and JOINs in Prolog. </span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The second part is a translation of the Social-Network quiz questions from </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-databases-relational-databases-and-sql-19468" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Databases: Relational Databases and SQL</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Stanford course. You’ll convert natural language questions into Prolog prompts.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The third part of the course is all about recursion, or in mathematical terms transitive closures. Here, you’ll also learn commands that are easy to do in Prolog but not in SQL, for example returning paths and guarding against endless cycles.</span></p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course consists of three parts. href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/udemy-top-courses/">[2023] अब तक के 250 शीर्ष Udemy कोर्स</a> दिखाई दिए पहले <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">क्लास सेंट्रल की रिपोर्ट</a> पर।</p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-73861" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses.png" alt="Udemy Top Courses" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/udemy">Udemy</a> is one of the largest online learning platforms for professional learning. <a href="https://about.udemy.com/">According to the company</a>, they have 57 million registered users. An <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/udemy-by-the-numbers/">analysis by Class Central</a> shows they’ve launched over 200,000 courses since 2010.</p> <p>The pandemic boosted the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/mooc-stats-pandemic/">fortune of many online providers</a>. Udemy was no exception. In 2020, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/the-second-year-of-the-mooc/">propelled by the pandemic</a>, they <a href="https://www.crunchbase.com/organization/udemy/company_financials">raised $123 million</a> and increased their valuation by over $1 billion.</p> <p>In 2022, the situation changed. Overall, the company raised ~$300 million at a valuation over <a href="https://www.businesswire.com/news/home/20201118005326/en/Udemy-Raises-50-Million-to-Fuel-Accelerated-Global-Demand-for-Online-Learning">$3 billion</a>. But Udemy&#8217;s market cap has significantly <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/2022-year-in-review/">fallen, like that of many other online course platforms</a>.</p> <p>In this course ranking, let&#8217;s explore the best of the best that Udemy has to offer.</p> <h2>Udemy By the Numbers</h2> <figure id="attachment_84875" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-84875" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1.png"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-84875" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1.png" alt="" width="1536" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-84875" class="wp-caption-text">Udemy By the Numbers (Jan 2023)</figcaption></figure> <p>Analyzing Udemy&#8217;s catalog with my colleague <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha">@Archisha</a>, we discovered that they currently have over 202,000 courses — which amounts to a 33% increase in the last 2 years. You may find a complete analysis of Udemy&#8217;s catalog here: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/udemy-by-the-numbers/">202K Courses, 662M Enrollments: Breaking Down Udemy’s Massive Catalog</a>.</p> <p>Combined, Udemy’s 202K courses have gathered ~662 million enrollments and average 3274 enrollments per course. What I found most surprising is that the median enrollment is only 240, which means that half of Udemy’s courses don’t reach 240 learners.</p> <p>Currently, there are 718 courses with over 100K enrollments and 4 courses with over a million enrollments.</p> <p>Do Udemy courses satisfy the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pareto_principle">Pareto 80/20 principle</a>? I found that Udemy’s top-20% courses by enrollment account for 91% of all enrollments.</p> <p>You can also find some of the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/udemy">best Udemy courses</a> on Class Central&#8217;s catalog page.</p> <hr /> <h2>250 Top Udemy Courses</h2> <p>Here&#8217;s a quick summary of 250 Udemy top courses based on the number of enrollments:</p> <ul> <li>Enrollments range from <strong>187K</strong> to <strong>1.8M</strong>. There are 4 courses with over <strong>1M</strong> enrollments.</li> <li>Combined, they account for <strong>79.5M</strong> enrollments, with an average of <strong>318K</strong> enrollments.</li> <li><strong>31%</strong> of the courses are free.</li> <li><strong>90%</strong> of the courses are in English.</li> <li aria-level="1">Combined, they represent <strong>4K</strong> hours of content.</li> </ul> <p>Without further ado, here are the top 250 courses on Udemy sorted by number of enrollments:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-java-tutorial-27747">Java Tutorial for Complete Beginners</a></li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-complete-python-bootcamp-23623">The Complete Python Bootcamp From Zero to Hero in Python</a></li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-microsoft-excel-2013-from-beginner-to-advan-24946">Microsoft Excel &#8211; मैं अपने कर्मचारियों को कैसा महसूस कराना चाहता हूं। यह कोर्स वह सब कुछ है जिससे किसी भी व्यवसाय के मालिक को गुजरना पड़ता है।</p> <p>इस पाठ्यक्रम के साथ, आपको वास्तव में अपने कर्मचारियों को जानने की आवश्यकता होगी: उन्हें कैसे रखा जाए और जब वे आपके लिए काम करते हैं तो उनके प्रदर्शन का मूल्यांकन कैसे करें; उन्हें अपनी प्रतिभा और उनकी राय पर चर्चा करने और दिखाने के लिए जगह देना वास्तव में एक व्यवसाय में मायने रखता है। मेरे पास हमेशा यह नारा है जिसका उपयोग मैं व्यापार मालिकों को सलाह देते समय करता हूं: "जिस तरह से आप अपने कर्मचारियों के साथ व्यवहार करते हैं वह उस दर को निर्धारित करेगा जिस पर वे आपके व्यवसाय को बढ़ाने में मदद करेंगे। 75% कर्मचारी हमेशा अपने नियोक्ता के व्यवसाय के लिए सकारात्मक परिणाम चाहते हैं, जबकि 25% केवल काम करना और वेतन अर्जित करना चाहते हैं, बिना इस बात पर ध्यान दिए कि व्यवसाय कैसे सफल होता है। अपने कर्मचारियों के साथ सही व्यवहार करने से आपके व्यवसाय को इस अर्थ में बचाने में मदद मिल सकती है कि कोई भी उस नौकरी को खोना नहीं चाहता जिसे वे महत्व देते हैं और सही व्यवहार प्राप्त करना चाहते हैं।</p> <div class="उद्धरण सापेक्ष पैडिंग-हॉर्ज़-लार्ज xबड़ा-अप-पैडिंग-हॉर्ज़-xxबड़ा पैडिंग-वर्ट-xxस्मॉल मार्जिन-बॉटम-लार्ज कोट-पुल कोट-टेक्स्ट"> <p>विवरणों पर ध्यान दें: जब कार्यस्थल सुविधाजनक होता है तो कर्मचारी विवरण और अपने वातावरण पर बहुत ध्यान देते हैं। </div> <p>निष्कर्ष निकालने के लिए, प्रत्येक व्यवसाय स्वामी को अपना उद्देश्य खोजने के लिए स्वयं की खोज शुरू करने की आवश्यकता है और उन्हें अपनी अपेक्षाओं पर भी काम करना चाहिए।</p> <h2><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/gs10kw-11222">अपना व्यवसाय बढ़ाएं</a></h2> <figure id="attachment_85291" JLPT N5, N4 and N3 grammar and vocabulary</span></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">What is Japanese (Language)?</span></h2> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japanese (日本語, Nihongo) is the native language primarily spoken by the people of Japan where it is the national language. Japanese belongs to the </span><a target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japonic_languages" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japonic</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> or Japanese-Ryukyuan language family.</span></p> <h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Hiragana, Katakana, and Kanji</span></h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Japanese language uses three scripts: Hiragana, Katakana, and Kanji. Let’s take a quick look at each of them.</span></p> <figure id="attachment_85263" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85263" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85263" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts.png" alt="" width="1537" height="769" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85263" class="wp-caption-text">The three scripts (<a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-learn-japanese-for-beginners-26156" rel="noopener">Learn Japanese for Beginners: The Ultimate 100-Lesson Course</a>)</figcaption></figure> <p><b>Hiragana</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> is used to write functional words and particles. Hiragana is like the basic Japanese alphabet and consists of 46 characters.</span></p> <p><b>Katakana</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> is used to write foreign words and names. Katakana is almost exactly the same as Hiragana with 46 characters except that it is written slightly differently.</span></p> <p><b>Kanji</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> is used to write native Japanese words or words of Chinese origin. Kanji characters represent an idea or concept and act more like entire words than individual letters. There are over 2,000 Kanji characters!</span></p> <h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japanese Proficiency Test: JLPT</span></h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.jlpt.jp/e/index.html" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japanese-Language Proficiency Test</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> (JLPT), offered by the Japan Foundation and Japan Educational Exchanges and Services, is the largest-scale Japanese-language test in the world. It is held worldwide to evaluate and certify proficiency in Japanese of non-native speakers. Language proficiency is tested on the basis of reading and listening, as well as vocabulary and grammar.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The JLPT has five levels, N1, N2, N3, N4 and N5, the level of difficulty increasing from N5 to N1. Below is a summary of the linguistic competence required for each level as described by </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.jlpt.jp/e/about/levelsummary.html" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">JLPT</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>N1</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand Japanese used in a variety of circumstances.</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>N2</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand Japanese used in everyday situations, and in a variety of circumstances to a certain degree.</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>N3</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand Japanese used in everyday situations to a certain degree.</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>N4</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand basic Japanese.</span></td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>N5</b></td> <td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand some basic Japanese.</span></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Why are Japanese Skills Important?</span></h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Among the </span><a target="_blank" href="https://joyofjapanese.com/why-learn-japanese/" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">many reasons to learn Japanese</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> there are a few that stand out: Being able to communicate with over 125 million native speakers (Japanese is the 8th </span><a target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_languages_by_number_of_native_speakers" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">most spoken language in the world</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">), enjoying one of the most popular cultures in the world with its unique cuisine, music and movie industry, and most importantly, animes in their original language. These are more than enough reasons to convince any language aficionado to get started learning Japanese. </span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In addition to that, Japan is also known for its tech and automobile industry, bringing to the world a number of </span><a target="_blank" href="https://blog.japanwondertravel.com/largest-and-popular-japanese-companies-34000" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">large Japanese companies</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> (such as Nintendo, Toyota, Canon, Sony, etc.) that carry in their core a strong culture attached to Japan roots.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">And lastly, if you want to open up to a number of opportunities as a Japanese translator or interpreter to your own language, there are hundreds of job openings on </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.indeed.com/q-Japanese-Translator-jobs.html?vjk=6566af5e8b50f060" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Indeed</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.upwork.com/freelance-jobs/translation-japanese-english/" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Upwork</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.linkedin.com/jobs/japanese-translator-jobs/?currentJobId=3307031894" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">LinkedIn</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">. You can also work as a language instructor or even diversify your reach as a tour guide and help Japanese travelers visiting your country.</span></p> <h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What is My Experience with Japanese?</span></h3> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I’ve learned a bit of Japanese mainly from anime, J-pop and Japanese movies. As my interest grew, I started learning more about Japan in general, so I became familiar with how Japanese actually works in the real world. Hearing real people talk gave me more enthusiasm to learn the language and explore the country as well.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Besides that, I am a </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.coursera.org/instructor/archisha-bhar" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Guided Project Instructor</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and a Beta Tester at Coursera, having tested many courses before they’re officially launched. I have taken </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">over 50 online courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> in various subjects.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My experience as an online learner and teacher has given me some perspective on what to look for in an online course. I used my experience to evaluate each course in this list.</span></p> <p><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79248 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2.png" alt="Find your next course on Class Central" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Course Ranking Methodology</span></h2> <p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology I used in previous rankings (</span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">you can find them all here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">). दिखाई दिए <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">क्लास सेंट्रल की रिपोर्ट</a>।</p> <p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85268" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Erlang-BCG-Banner.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" GoDaddy. IBM. Heroku. What do they all have in common?</p> <p>They all use Erlang in their technology stack!</p> <p>Erlang is a programming language specifically designed for building scalable, fault-tolerant systems that can run smoothly in a distributed environment. Its unique approach to concurrency and message-passing makes it ideal for building real-time, high-traffic systems like WhatsApp&#8217;s messaging platform, Cisco&#8217;s networking equipment, GoDaddy&#8217;s hosting services, IBM&#8217;s cloud offerings, and Heroku&#8217;s platform as a service. In fact, <a href="https://erlang-companies.org/companies/cisco.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">90% of all internet traffic goes through Erlang controlled nodes</a>.</p> <p>Want to find out and learn more about this (kind of) unknown yet powerful language? Continue reading to see my picks for the best Erlang courses. The team needed a programming language that can handle <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telephone_exchange" target="_blank" rel="noopener">telephone switching</a> — a very difficult endeavor that requires high levels of concurrency and zero downtime (I’m sure you can imagine why).</p> <p>After experimenting with dozens of different languages, they came to a stark conclusion: no such language exists! Instead of giving up or settling for compromises, they instead decided to create their own programming language.</p> <p>Hopefully that brief history lesson gave you some context for why Erlang is known for two things: its practical concurrent programming and its robust virtual machine.</p> <p>Erlang is a functional programming language for all the right reasons — scalability and concurrency. It has a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Actor_model" target="_blank" rel="noopener">lightweight threading model</a> (which Rust also uses) and a powerful process-based runtime system. <a href="https://erlang.org/course/history.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Companies like WhatsApp and Heroku</a> are able to scale and handle millions of concurrent connections in real-time thanks to Erlang.</p> <p>Also, the Erlang virtual machine (BEAM) is legendary for its fault-tolerance. The language has built-in support for handling failures, like automatically restarting processes and recovering from crashes. For mission-critical systems, you can be rest assured that your applications will continue running 24/7 even when things eventually go wrong.</p> <p>In addition to its concurrency and fault tolerance features, Erlang is also a highly expressive language that allows you to write concise and elegant code. It has a simple syntax and a rich set of libraries, like the Open Telecom Platform, making it easy to learn and use.</p> <p>Unfortunately, there are not enough developers in the world that know Erlang, even though Erlang developers are highly sought after. That’s why Erlang is the second highest paying programming language to learn (after Clojure) according to the <a href="https://survey.stackoverflow.co/2022/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Stack Overflow Developer Survey 2022</a>. So why not become one of them? Whether you&#8217;re building a web application, a real-time messaging system, or a distributed database, Erlang is a worthy choice for building reliable, scalable systems.</p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79247 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png" alt="Find your next course." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <h2>Best Courses Guides Methodology</h2> <p>I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous Best Courses Guides (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">you can find them all here</a>). further ado, let’s go through the top picks.</p> <h2 id="anchor-1">1. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-erlang-tutorial-120161" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang Tutorial (Erlang Tutorial)</a></h2> <p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85269" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Erlang-Tutorial-Erlang-Tutorial.png" to learn Erlang is the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-erlang-tutorial-120161" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i>Erlang Tutorial</i></a> playlist.</p> <p>I chose this course as my top pick because it is both recent and comprehensive. Plus, the video tutorials teach Erlang through interactive programming and examples. By the end of this tutorial, you’ll have a well-grounded understanding of the Erlang programming language.</p> <p>Some prior knowledge of programming is required to take this course.</p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p>In this tutorial, you’ll start by learning the tools and vocabulary of the Erlang programming language. You’ll write a simple &#8220;Hello, World&#8221; module and compile it to get a feel for the Erlang syntax and structure. You’ll then delve into common programming concepts such as data types, control structures, and functions, but with a functional and concurrent twist specific to Erlang.</p> <p>One of the key features of Erlang is its use of processes to execute code concurrently (fun fact, millions of processes can run at the same time!). You’ll learn how to spawn and manage them. Other functional programming concepts will be explored too, such as recursion, anonymous functions, and higher-order functions. Along with other concepts like atoms, comprehensions, and pattern matching, you’ll have the skills to write efficient and scalable code.</p> <p>In addition to these foundational topics, you’ll study more advanced constructs in Erlang. You’ll learn how to use maps and processes together to build a simple key-value database that can perform basic data operations. You’ll also learn about error handling in Erlang, and how to design your code to continue running even when errors occur. And to give you some practical examples, you’ll implement a palindrome checker and Conway&#8217;s game of life in Erlang, giving you the opportunity to apply your knowledge to real-world problems.</p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p>This course is 8–9 hours long. You’ll learn by watching the lecture videos and following along with the instructor as he codes interactively using the Erlang shell.</p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>Channel</b></td> <td>Erlang (University of Kent)</a></h2> <p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85270" best Erlang course are <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-erlang-master-classes-120166" target="_blank" rel="noopener">the Erlang Master Classes</a> from the University of Kent.</p> <p>This <b>free</b> course comprises three master classes taught by esteemed Erlang programmers (one of them even helped invent Erlang). Each class focuses on different aspects of Erlang — functional programming, concurrent programming, and larger-scale programming with OTP — are used to solve complex real-world problems through case studies and examples. By the end of the course, you’ll know how Erlang is used practically.</p> <p>The course assumes you have some basic familiarity with Erlang (watch the first video of the first masterclass to know more).</p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p>The first master class focuses on language processing in general, with a focus on processing arithmetical expressions in Erlang. This will include how to interpret, compile, and run the expressions on a virtual machine, as well as simplifying and converting them to and from a textual form.</p> <p>In the second master class, you’ll understand how Erlang does concurrent programming in Erlang through the ‘share nothing’ concurrency model. You’ll learn how to make sequential code concurrent and how to build systems using communicating processes. You’ll also cover Erlang’s famous approach to fault tolerance and how errors can happen while still keeping the program running.</p> <p>Erlang has a wide ecosystem of tools and libraries — that’s what makes Erlang great. But, the most important tool for servers is arguably the The Open Telecom Platform (OTP). Hence in the final master class, you’ll explore OTP in depth, taking a look at its generic behaviors (such as a generic server) and how it can be used to build complex systems quickly and reliably, in addition to packaging and releasing systems.</p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p>The master classes are presented by Joe Armstrong, Ericsson AB and KTH, Stockholm, and one of the inventors of Erlang; Francesco Cesarini, CTO and founder of Erlang Solutions Ltd; and Simon Thompson, functional programming teacher and researcher at the University of Kent. Each Master Class ends with a discussion between the three presenters on some of the issues raised by the Master Class.</p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>Institution</b></td> <td>University of Kent</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Instructors</b></td> <td>Joe Armstrong, Francesco Cesarini, Simon Thompson</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Level</b></td> <td>Intermediate</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Workload</b></td> <td>4 hours</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Certificate</b></td> <td>None</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h3>Fun Facts</h3> <ul> <li aria-level="1">This MOOC was created to celebrate the university&#8217;s 50th anniversary. By the end, you’ll be able to build a system that uses functional concurrent programming to achieve scalability and reliability while still being easy to understand, debug, and maintain.</p> <p>You’ll need basic programming knowledge and a MacOS or Linux system to take this course.</p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p>The course starts by introducing you to the Erlang Shell, where you can get hands-on experience with the language by evaluating expressions and compiling modules. Then, you’ll delve into the world of functional programming in Erlang, including concepts such as pattern-matching and recursion. You’ll see how these functional programming techniques can be combined with concurrent programming to take advantage of Erlang&#8217;s efficient concurrency model using message-passing processes.</p> <p>Next, you’ll cover how to handle errors in your Erlang program, both sequentially and concurrently, to ensure that it can continue running smoothly even in the face of unexpected issues. You’ll also learn about OTP that provides a powerful library and tools for building distributed systems. Finally, the course explores modern Erlang development practices and introduces you to Rebar3, a popular build and package management tool for Erlang.</p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p>This course is 4 hours long. You’ll learn by watching the lecture videos chapter-by-chapter, with each chapter ending with a summary.</p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>Provider</b></td> <td>CodeRed</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Instructor</b></td> <td>Brujo Benavides Rodriguez</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Level</b></td> <td>Beginner</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Workload</b></td> <td>4 hours</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Certificate</b></td> <td>Paid</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h3>Fun Facts</h3> <ul> <li aria-level="1">Brujo Benavides Rodriguez is a long-time Erlang developer and trainer. He is a maintainer of multiple open-source projects and a member of the Education Working Group at the EEF. He has also worked as a trainer for 5 years at Inaka and Erlang Solutions, delivering Erlang lessons to individuals and teams around the world.</li> </ul> <p>If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-introduction-to-erlang-programming-120167" target="_blank" rel="noopener">more information about the course and how to enroll here</a>.</p> <h2 id="anchor-4">4. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-learn-you-some-erlang-120165" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn You Some Erlang for Great Good! (Frederic Trottier-Hebert)</a></h2> <p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85272" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Learn-You-Some-Erlang-for-Great-Good-Frederic-Trottier-Hebert.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Learn-You-Some-Erlang-for-Great-Good-Frederic-Trottier-Hebert.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Learn-You-Some-Erlang-for-Great-Good-Frederic-Trottier-Hebert-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Learn-You-Some-Erlang-for-Great-Good-Frederic-Trottier-Hebert-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-learn-you-some-erlang-120165" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn You Some Erlang for Great Good!</a> is a <b>free</b> comprehensive text-based Erlang tutorial, based on another well-received tutorial of similar name, <a href="http://learnyouahaskell.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn You a Haskell for Great Good!</a>.</p> <p>It is for people who have basic knowledge of programming in imperative languages but are unfamiliar with functional programming. You’ll explore how Erlang is very pragmatic in its approach to functional programming, and how it results in robust, concurrent, distributed systems.</p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p>You’ll start by exploring the basics of the language, like variables, data types, and conditional statements. And since the language follows the functional paradigm, you’ll learn how to solve problems the functional way, using concepts like recursion and higher order functions.</p> <p>Next, you’ll delve into the concepts of concurrency in Erlang and learn how to use processes, message passing, and other techniques to build concurrent systems. You’ll also learn about OTP (Open Telecom Platform), a set of libraries and tools for building distributed and fault-tolerant systems in Erlang. And this fault-tolerance can only be resolved through smart error and exception handling.</p> <p>Data structures and algorithms appear everywhere in software, and Erlang is no exception. You’ll use them to solve common problems. You’ll also learn about working with sockets and networking, along with event handlers and supervisors.</p> <p>Finally, you’ll learn about testing and debugging in Erlang, including how to use tools such as EUnit to test your code and how to release and deploy Erlang applications.</p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p>This tutorial consists of 36 chapters. You’ll learn by reading through the many chapters and implementing the code given in the course on your system.</p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>Website</b></td> <td>learnyousomeerlang.com</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Instructor</b></td> <td>Frederic Trottier-Hebert</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Level</b></td> <td>Beginner</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Workload</b></td> <td>N/A</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Certificate</b></td> <td>None</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h3>Fun Facts</h3> <ul> <li aria-level="1">Frederic Trottier-Hebert is a French-Canadian working as a site reliability engineer at honeycomb.io. He owns a <a href="https://ferd.ca/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">blog</a>.</li> <li aria-level="1">He has also written other books / tutorials like &#8216;Erlang in Anger&#8217; and &#8216;Property Based Testing with PropEr, Erlang, and Elixir&#8217;.</li> </ul> <p>If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-learn-you-some-erlang-120165" target="_blank" rel="noopener">more information about the course and how to enroll here</a>.</p> <h2 id="anchor-5">5. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-erlang-logo-an-erlang-course-120164" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang University (erlang.org)</a></h2> <p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85273" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-Erlang-University-erlang.org_.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-Erlang-University-erlang.org_.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-Erlang-University-erlang.org_-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-Erlang-University-erlang.org_-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-erlang-logo-an-erlang-course-120164" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang University</a> is the official Erlang course from the Ericsson OTP Team. This <b>free</b> text-based course covers Erlang from its history, to the basics parts of Erlang as well as to the advanced.</p> <p>However, this course is quite bare, so be sure to supplement this course with other courses, the <a href="https://erlang.org/course/exercises.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">course’s own exercises</a>, and <a href="https://erlangforums.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang’s discussion forums</a>.</p> <p>Programming experience is needed to take this course.</p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p>This course is divided into 5 modules.</p> <p>First, you’ll take a short look at the history of Erlang to understand and appreciate the motivations and design principles behind its creation. Then, you’ll start with the basics of sequential programming which follows the style of many other languages where code is run on a single thread. This will include learning basic programming concepts as well as Erlang’s functional programming capabilities.</p> <p>Next, you’ll get to the exciting part of Erlang: concurrent programming. You’ll understand how to use processes, lightweight concurrent units of execution that can run alongside other processes. You’ll also learn how errors can propagate through processes and how to handle them when they occur. Lastly, the course ends by covering a few tricky topics and quirks in the Erlang language.</p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p>According to the course description, this course will take 4 days to complete, but that can vary depending on your current skill. You’ll learn by reading through the course modules and completing the exercises to help you put into practice what you’ve learned.</p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>Provider</b></td> <td>erlang.org</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Level</b></td> <td>Beginner</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Workload</b></td> <td>N/A</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Certificate</b></td> <td>None</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <p>If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-erlang-logo-an-erlang-course-120164" target="_blank" rel="noopener">more information about the course and how to enroll here</a>.</p> <h2 id="anchor-6">6. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-modern-erlang-for-beginners-120163" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Modern Erlang for Beginners (Roberto Ostinelli)</a></h2> <p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85274" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Modern-Erlang-for-Beginners-Roberto-Ostinelli.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Modern-Erlang-for-Beginners-Roberto-Ostinelli.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Modern-Erlang-for-Beginners-Roberto-Ostinelli-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Modern-Erlang-for-Beginners-Roberto-Ostinelli-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-modern-erlang-for-beginners-120163" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Modern Erlang for Beginners</a> is a <b>paid </b>Udemy course that provides a simple and concise introduction to Erlang.</p> <p>To take this course, you should have some experience with another programming language.</p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p>You’ll begin by installing and setting up Erlang on your PC, using the IntelliJ IDE. Then, you’ll learn Erlang basics, especially how to think in Erlang, like variables, control structures, data types, and data structure, as well as taking a careful look at functions, guards, and patterns in the context of functional programming.</p> <p>Erlang is known for its ability to handle concurrent processing, and you’ll learn how it achieves this through processes, messages, and other techniques to build distributed systems. To further illustrate these concepts, you’ll examine a real-world example of a bank system. Finally, you’ll explore how to improve the bank example using the tools and libraries provided by the Open Telecom Platform (OTP) and learn best practices for Erlang development.</p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p>This course is 3–4 hours long. You’ll learn by watching the lecture videos, taking notes of the code examples, and completing the course exercises.</p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>Provider</b></td> <td>Udemy</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Instructor</b></td> <td>Roberto Ostinelli</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Level</b></td> <td>Beginner</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Workload</b></td> <td>3–4 hours</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Enrollments</b></td> <td>655</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Rating</b></td> <td>4.6 / 5.0 (157)</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Certificate</b></td> <td>Paid</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h3>Fun Facts</h3> <ul> <li aria-level="1">Roberto Ostinelli is an experienced software developer with over a decade of professional experience using Erlang. It is a <b>free </b>online coding platform that not only offers a variety of programming challenges and exercises for all skill levels, but it also provides a <b>free </b>mentoring service where you can request personalized feedback from experienced Erlang programmers for a particularly challenging exercise.</p> <h3>What You’ll Learn</h3> <p>The course consists of three difficulties: easy, medium, and hard.</p> <p>Easy exercises consist of tasks like determining the geometric type of a triangle, finding the prime factors of a number, and implementing basic lists operations.</p> <p>For medium difficulty exercises, you’ll calculate the date of meetups, add numbers to a  minesweeper board, and detect saddle points in a matrix.</p> <p>Hard exercises include creating a zipper for a binary tree, returning a square matrix of a number in spiral order, and making a chain of dominoes.</p> <h3>How You’ll Learn</h3> <p>This course is self-paced, so you can take all the time you need to complete the 70+ hands-on programming exercises. Each exercise comes with automatic feedback of your code as well as personal mentoring to help you understand your code’s strengths and flaws.</p> <table> <tbody> <tr> <td><b>Provider</b></td> <td>Exercism</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Level</b></td> <td>All levels</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Workload</b></td> <td>N/A</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Enrollments</b></td> <td>32K</td> </tr> <tr> <td><b>Certificate</b></td> <td>None</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h3>Fun Facts</h3> <ul> <li aria-level="1">Exercism provides exercises on 50+ programming languages like Python, Kotlin, F#, and even WebAssembly.</li> <li aria-level="1">Their mission is to help everyone get really good at programming, regardless of their background, share the love of programming, and help people upskill as part of their upward social mobility.</li> <li aria-level="1">Around 60 people have contributed towards the Erlang syllabus and exercises, with over 60 mentors available at the time of writing.</li> </ul> <p>If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exercism-erlang-110593" target="_blank" rel="noopener">more information about the course and how to enroll here</a>.</p> <p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-erlang-courses/">7 Best Erlang Courses to Take in 2023</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p> हत्तपः://ववव.क्लाससेंट्रल.कॉम/रिपोर्ट/बेस्ट-ेरलंग-कोर्सेज/फीड/ 0
